# Programme Taxonomy Gaps

## National University of Singapore (2026-07-13)

Research owner: `codex-luna-nus-20260713`

The following current NUS offerings were verified from the official undergraduate programme
catalogue or AY2026/27 Bulletin but were not force-mapped because the approved registry has no
exact canonical programme at the same level or because the official interdisciplinary award would
be materially narrowed by an existing slug. Exact matches published in the NUS catalogue payload
are not repeated here.

| University | Country | University slug | Exact official programme title | Official award | Level | Proposed canonical name | Proposed slug | Primary-source URL | Why existing taxonomy does not fit | Agent ID | Status |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| National University of Singapore | Singapore | national-university-of-singapore | Business Administration | Bachelor of Business Administration / undergraduate business degree | bachelors | Bachelor's in Business Administration | bachelors-business-administration | https://nus.edu.sg/oam/undergraduate-programmes | The active registry has no undergraduate business/management canonical; MBA and postgraduate business slugs would misstate the qualification level. | codex-luna-nus-20260713 | proposed |
| National University of Singapore | Singapore | national-university-of-singapore | Business Analytics | Bachelor of Science / undergraduate programme | bachelors | Bachelor's in Business Analytics | bachelors-business-analytics | https://nus.edu.sg/oam/undergraduate-programmes | The registry has M.Sc. Business Analytics but no approved bachelor's-level Business Analytics slug; mapping to the master's category would be inaccurate. | codex-luna-nus-20260713 | proposed |
| National University of Singapore | Singapore | national-university-of-singapore | Computer Engineering | Bachelor of Engineering | bachelors | Bachelor's in Computer Engineering | bachelor-computer-engineering | https://www.nus.edu.sg/nusbulletin/ay202627/programmes/college-of-design-and-engineering/undergraduate-education/ | The active engineering registry has Computer Science and Engineering but no distinct Computer Engineering canonical; collapsing the official electrical/computing engineering degree into CSE would lose its identity. | codex-luna-nus-20260713 | proposed |
| National University of Singapore | Singapore | national-university-of-singapore | Data Science and Economics | Bachelor of Science (Honours), cross-disciplinary programme | bachelors | Bachelor's in Data Science and Economics | bachelors-data-science-economics | https://www.nus.edu.sg/nusbulletin/ay202627/programmes/faculty-of-science/undergraduate-education/ | The registry has bachelor's Economics and postgraduate Data Science, but no exact cross-disciplinary undergraduate Data Science and Economics canonical. | codex-luna-nus-20260713 | proposed |
| National University of Singapore | Singapore | national-university-of-singapore | Environmental Studies | Bachelor of Environmental Studies (Honours) | bachelors | Bachelor's in Environmental Studies | bachelor-environmental-studies | https://www.nus.edu.sg/nusbulletin/ay202627/programmes/faculty-of-science/undergraduate-education/ | The registry has Environmental Science but not the distinct interdisciplinary Environmental Studies award; mapping it to Environmental Science would misstate the degree. | codex-luna-nus-20260713 | proposed |
| National University of Singapore | Singapore | national-university-of-singapore | Pharmaceutical Science | Bachelor of Science (Honours) | bachelors | Bachelor's in Pharmaceutical Science | bachelor-pharmaceutical-science | https://www.nus.edu.sg/nusbulletin/ay202627/programmes/faculty-of-science/undergraduate-education/ | The registry has Bachelor of Pharmacy and integrated Master of Pharmacy, but no Pharmaceutical Science bachelor's canonical; those professional pharmacy categories are not equivalent. | codex-luna-nus-20260713 | proposed |
| National University of Singapore | Singapore | national-university-of-singapore | Philosophy, Politics and Economics | Bachelor of Arts (Honours), cross-disciplinary programme | bachelors | Bachelor's in Philosophy, Politics and Economics | bachelor-philosophy-politics-economics | https://nus.edu.sg/oam/undergraduate-programmes | The registry has individual philosophy, political-science and economics categories but no exact PPE cross-disciplinary canonical; selecting one would omit two-thirds of the award. | codex-luna-nus-20260713 | proposed |
| National University of Singapore | Singapore | national-university-of-singapore | Engineering | Bachelor of Engineering | bachelors | Bachelor's in General Engineering | bachelor-general-engineering | https://www.nus.edu.sg/nusbulletin/ay202627/programmes/college-of-design-and-engineering/undergraduate-education/ | NUS publishes a broad Engineering entry route alongside named disciplines; the registry only has discipline-level engineering slugs, so no exact generic Engineering degree mapping was approved. | codex-luna-nus-20260713 | proposed |


Research owner: `019f5523-3eb6-7c21-8256-e0d88b1532c6` (Codex University of Bremen run)
Reviewed: 2026-07-12

These official University of Bremen programmes were verified as legitimate current offerings but
were held because the approved registry has no exact canonical match. No programme below was
force-mapped to a merely similar engineering or business category.

## Saarland taxonomy review correction — 2026-07-12

The expanded global registry made the following previously appended Saarland proposals exact
matches. They are superseded as taxonomy gaps and are published through the Saarland payload where
the programme has complete current source coverage: Chemistry (B.Sc.), Mathematics (B.Sc.), Physics
(B.Sc.), Psychology (B.Sc.), History (B.A.), Philosophy (B.A.), Chemistry (M.Sc.), Mathematics
(M.Sc.), Physics (M.Sc.) and Psychology (M.Sc.). The remaining Saarland rows above remain proposed
gaps unless separately mapped in a later validated payload.

## University of Ottawa — 2026–27 portfolio review

These current official catalogue offerings were researched but held because no exact approved
canonical mapping exists. The published Ottawa payload contains only exact matches; no title below
was force-mapped to a nearby discipline. Source bundle: the official [2026–27 undergraduate
catalogue](https://catalogue.uottawa.ca/en/undergrad/undergrad.pdf), [2026–27 graduate
catalogue](https://catalogue.uottawa.ca/en/graduate/graduate.pdf), and [official programme
catalogue](https://catalogue.uottawa.ca/en/programs/), checked 2026-07-12.

|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|

## Dalhousie University — 12 July 2026

The official Dalhousie catalogue was rechecked on 2026-07-12. The offerings below are legitimate
current degree-bearing titles, but the approved registry has no exact canonical match. They were not
force-mapped to a broad neighbouring discipline. Dalhousie's MD, PharmD and direct-entry BScN are
separate evidence-based audience/restriction holds, not taxonomy gaps.

## Carleton University — 12 July 2026

The official Carleton 2026–27 undergraduate and graduate calendars were reviewed in full at the
program-family level. The payload publishes only exact approved mappings and preserves the existing
Carleton BScN. The offerings below are legitimate current catalogue entries held because the
approved registry has no exact canonical, because the award is a graduate diploma/certificate or
collaborative specialization rather than a standalone degree, or because mapping to a neighbouring
discipline would erase a materially different curriculum or award.

| University | Country | University slug | Exact official programme title | Official award | Level | Proposed canonical name | Proposed slug | Primary-source URL | Why existing taxonomy does not fit | Agent id | Status |

## Université de Montréal (2026-07-12)

- Official title: `Diplôme d'études supérieures spécialisées en études internationales`
  - Award/level: DESS / postgraduate diploma, 30 credits
  - Primary source: https://admission.umontreal.ca/programmes/dess-en-etudes-internationales/program-structure/
  - Proposed canonical: `dess-international-relations`
  - Mismatch: the approved registry has master's international relations but no exact postgraduate diploma-level international-relations programme; do not force-map to the master's.
- Official title: `Maîtrise en affaires publiques et internationales (MAPI)`
  - Award/level: master's, 45 credits, required professional internship; concentrations in diplomacy and international affairs, political journalism and communication, and public policy
  - Primary source: https://cerium.umontreal.ca/etudes/programmes/
  - Proposed canonical: `master-public-affairs-international-relations`
- Mismatch: the approved registry has international relations, public policy and communication masters separately, but no exact interdisciplinary public-affairs-and-international-relations award; do not force-map to one of those narrower programmes.
